| <span data-ttu-id="6b3c1-1954">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6b3c1-1954">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="6b3c1-1955">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6b3c1-1955">Value</span></span> |
